(light crossbow +1). Special defense: fanaticism. Possessions: Set armor (see Arden Vul items) and wooden shield; footman’s mace +1; spear; light crossbow +1 with 20 bolts.

### 4-47: Overseer

* Belisarius the Overseer, secondmost in the cult of Set, lives and works in this large room.
	* The chamber is divided into a public and private areas.
		* Private area (east): shielded by some painted wooden screens.
			* A simple bed, an armoire, a writing desk, a weapon and armor rack, a practice dummy, two cots for the aides, a set of four easy chairs around a coffee table, and a cabinet containing 22 bottles of excellent brandy.
		* Public area
			* A large tactical table on which lie various maps.
				* Maps (incomplete) of the northern and southern caves of Level 4.
				* One ancient map of portions of the lower levels (GM’s choice).
			* Several writing desks and chairs containing roster lists, personnel reports, logistical reports, and so forth.
		* North wall
			* Next to the door to the caves is a large cabinet with a sizable number of curios looted from the halls, as well as 12 bound codices (on theological, military, and motivational subjects).
			* The north door leads to a narrow tunnel providing Belisarius with private access to the cavern (4-66) via a one-way door.
				* He doesn’t use this door often, so the corridor is thick with dust.
		* Secret Door (east, locked, key is hidden in the liquor cabinet): leads to a set of secret interrogation chambers.
			* Only the overseer and his aides-de-camp know of this door and the interrogation chambers.

* Two aides-de-camp (from the Alpha Sept) are always present in the public area.
* 50% chance Belisarius is present in his quarters.
	* Otherwise , typically in 4-2, 4-3, 4-7, 4-43, 4-51, 4-53, or 4-61.
	* 25% chance to be in 4-48 whenever the second mystery is performed.

* Belisarius the Overseer is the ranking ‘secular’ figure and second most powerful indivudal in the cult of Set.
	* The overseer is in charge of all guardsmen, military expeditions, security, patrols, and so forth.
	* Belisarius is a devout, even fanatical, follower of Set, and an adept politician.
	* In addition to his administrative skills, Belisarius is a formidable warrior.
	* He is also a misogynist and dislikes High Priestess Stephania intensely.
		* He is constantly plotting her demise, and hopes to replace her with the third priest, Lacedaion.
		* Stephania is aware of these machinations.  She has not acted against Belisarius yet solely because he is so good at what he does.
	* Despite his prejudices, Belisarius would never act to undermine the cult as a whole; only if he were convinced of the motives of outsiders would he consider employing them against Stephania.

Belisarius the Overseer, 7th-level male Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL LE; AC 2; MV 120’; HD 7; HP 70; #AT 3/2; Dmg 3-8 (javelin +2) or 4-11 (long sword +2). Abilities: STR 17, INT 13, WIS 16, DEX 11, CON 16, CHA 15. Possessions: chain mail +3; returning javelin +2 (see new magic items), long sword +2; potion of extra healing (x2); potion of fly; and a key-ring with keys to SL8-1 and 4-106. 

2 aides-de-camp, 3rd-level female Archontean fighters: SZ M; AL NE; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 3; HP 25, 22; #AT 1; Dmg 1-8 (mace), 1-6 (spear) or 1-4 (light crossbow). Possessions: Set armor (see Arden Vul items); spear; mace, and light crossbow.

### 4-48: 2nd Mystery of Set: Sandstorms and Scorpions

* This massive spherical chamber, 30' radius, houses the second of the Mysteries of Set.
	* The lower half of the sphere is filled with sand.
		* Buried at the bottom of the sphere is a locked strongbox.  Stephania and the modern cult of Set are ignorant of its existence.
			* 7,000 ancient gold solidi; an extra key to 4-106; a cleric scroll (the long death, warding chain of glyphs; both new); a silver ankh-key (av items).
	* The upper half is painted bright blue, with a large yellow sun in the center, enchanted with continual light.
	* Slender bridges (7’ wide, 5' above the sand) lead from doors in the north, south, and east sides of the sphere to meet in the center atop a 10’-radius circular platform (itself a pillar descending to the floor).
	* To the west is another platform and door leading to the chapel (4-61).
		* Here that Stephania performs the daily mystery.

The Second Mystery
* The second great mystery of the Set cult is performed here once per day.
	* Only important cultists are permitted to witness the summoning and taming of the desert storms.  The rest of the time, the doors to the chamber are kept locked.
* The Mystery of Storms
	* Celebrants enter through one of the doors and congregate on the central platform.
	* At precisely noon, Stephania (or another upper-circle priest) appears on the western platform accompanied by a drugged slave (or naughty acolyte).
	* She shouts the ritual words in the secret tongue of the priests of Set: 
		* “Set is spawned from the desert sands, hardy and severe. Let our hearts seek the discipline of the desert as we achieve his ends!” Applause is expected.
		* “When angered, Set looses his fury like the desert storm! Let those who cannot endure, perish!”
		* She kicks the victim onto the sands below, and, as the giant scorpions emerge to feast, she uses her rod of wind control (new) to produce a small but impressive sandstorm.  The entire chamber (save Stephania’s platform) is racked with howling wind and blowing sand for 2 full minutes.
			* During this performance, it is not uncommon for Set cultists on the main platform to settle old scores by pushing rivals into the maelstrom.
		* After two minutes, Stephania shouts in Archontean, in an enhanced voice that echoes through the winds, “For those who pursue his will, Lord Set eases their way, just as he tames the desert storms!  Speak your pleas!”
			* Those who ask a question into the winds may receive the a divination whispered in their ear, if their intent pleases Set.  Those who's aims  displease him receive a chilling warning or threat.
			* Celebrants often compete to purchase the victim to be sacrificed, as this gesture improves their odds of receiving guidance.
		* The winds cease and the chamber returns to normal. Celebrants are likely to witness the giant scorpions finishing off the sacrifice and anyone else who has fallen to the sands.

3 giant scorpions: SZ M; AL N; AC 3; MV 150’; HD 5+5; HP 42, 39, 35; #AT 3; Dmg 1-10/1-10/1-4. Special attacks: poison.
* Each scorpion wears a long necklace of gold (2,000 gp each).

Stephania: see 4-51

A human slave, noncombatant (AC 10, HP 3)

1-11 Set cultists (see new monsters): SZ M; AL LE; AC 9; MV 90’; HD 1; HP 7, 6, 5(x3), 4(x3), 3(x3); #AT 1; Dmg 1-4 (dagger) or 2-7 (flail) or 1-6 (staff). Special attacks: fanaticism. Possessions: padded armor; daggers; flails or staves.

Belisarius (25% chance, he loves this mystery); see 4-47.

### 4-49: Deacons’ Quarters

* These eleven 10’x10’ rooms are quarters for the deacons of the cult of Set.
	* Each contains a bed, a waste bucket, a writing desk, and a chest for clothes.
		* Somewhere in their chamber, each deacon has 10-100 sp, and a potion and/or clerical scroll (25% for each).
	* 10% chance to encounter a deacon at home, most of the time they are busy elsewhere within or without the complex.

1 Set deacon (see new monsters), as a 6th-level Archontean cleric of Set (10% chance): SZ M; AL LE; AC 3; MV 90’; HD 6; HP 42; #AT 1; Dmg 3-8 (mace +1).
* Possessions: Set armor +1 (see Arden Vul items); deacon’s was stick (see new magic items); footman’s mace +1; an amulet of protection against normal missiles (see new magic items); a potion of extra healing; a potion of glibness; a scroll of holy name (see new spells); and a gold holy symbol of Set (150 gp).
* Spells prayed for: command, cure light wounds (x2), cause fear, protection from good; chant, hold person, holy name (see new spells), know alignment, silence 15’ radius; animate dead, dispel magic, cause blindness; cause serious wounds.

### 4-50: Dormitory of the Acolytes

* A chaotic room crammed with ten triple bunk beds for the acolytes of the cult.
	* 30 unlocked wooden chests stowed are under the lowest bunks.
		* Each chest has a 50% chance for 3d6 sp in small coins.
	* The place smells strongly due to the sardine-like nature of the living conditions.
	* At any given moment 5 acolytes are present and asleep.

5 Set acolytes (see new monsters), as 3rd-level Archontean clerics of Set: SZ M; AL LE; AC 4; MV 60’; HD 3; HP 22, 20, 19, 18, 17; #AT 1; Dmg 2-7 (mace) and 1-4 (light crossbow). 
* Possessions: Set armor (see Arden Vul items); footman’s mace; light crossbow; acolyte’s was stick (see new magic items); and a silver holy symbol of Set (10 gp).
* Spells prayed for: command, cure light wounds, curse (reverse of bless), protection from good; hold person, silence 15’ radius.

### 4-51: High Priestess Stephania

* Stephania, the high priestess and Set pontifex, lives and works in this chamber.
	* The northern two-thirds are set up for public business. 
		* A sitting area with four wooden chairs around a coffee table.
			* Two silver ewers (35 gp each) are filled with wine (one always poisoned, well known to her confidants and enemies) and a set of 6 delicate crystal wine glasses (20 gp each).
		* A writing desk and a scroll cabinet occupy the western wall.
			* Her rod of wind control (new) usually rests on the writing table.
		* A portion of living mosaic (new) is set in the north wall, left of the door, showing the forum area (4-2).
		* Right of the door, a rack holds her red Set armor +2 (av items) and mace +3.
			* Note: Armor, mace, and rod of wind control present only if Stephania is here, else they are on her person.
	* The southern third of the room is set off by a pair of painted wooden screens, behind which is her living area.
		* A sumptuous feather bed, an armoire filled with robes, a set of sealed jars of water (she fears poison), a dressing table with makeup (15 gp), a stuffed leather chair, a beautiful red and gold carpet (100 gp), and a solid brass bust of a horned entity resting on a slender side table.
			* Bbrass devil’s head: an infernal effigy (new), keyed to a styx devil named Trasbellix. It's name is on a slip of parchment pinned to the rug's bottom.
			* Armoire (secret compartment): 10 perfect pearls (100 gp each), written testimony about Belisarius’s machinations, and substantial dirt on the Guild of Service.
				* Testimony from Yellup (a now dead source) describing the hatred of Belisarius (4-47) towards Stephania and the overseer’s secret efforts to persuade Lacedaion (4-57) to undermine Stephania’s rule.
				* A report (unnamed source) describing the daily activities of Gunnar, chief of the Guild of Service (4-10) over the past month.
					* The first week's entries show him energetically visiting every corner of the Guild’s area, consulting guildmasters, and generally acting frequently in public.
					* The last three weeks contain the same entry: “Stayed in his chamber and consulted with his advisors”. (A clue that Gunnar has been replaced by a doppelganger, see 4-10).
		* Heavy gold drapes hang on the south wall, behind which is a secret door.
			* Secret door (to 4-51a, locked, -15% to pick, Stephania holds the key).
		* On the east wall is a tapestry depicting an enormous Set animal.
			* Secret Door (to 4-52): small (4’ tall), opened by pushing a small floor tile while simultaneously pushing the door panel inward.

* 33% chance Stephania is present here.
	* 25% chance she is conducting a ritual in 4-61, else moving about the Set complex.
	* Once per day she presides over the second mystery (4-48). 
	* Whenever she is outside her chamber, she wears her Set armor +2 (av items) and carries her mace +3. 

* Stephania is a powerful cleric and a formidable adversary; indeed, her rise to the top of the Set hierarchy attests to her skill as a politician and a ruthless opponent. 
	* She is a petite, round woman with flaming red-hair (which helped her rise to power).
	* Naturally sallow, she only appears in public in elaborate make-up: she chalks her face white and accentuates her black eyes and brows.
* She always wears Batzas, one of the three rings of Set (new), her boots of the ogre (new), her pontifex’s was stick (new), and her necklace of missiles.
	* Her key ring has keys to most door locks in the compound, including the sole key to 4-51a, one of the few keys to SL8-1 (aka EX-16), and one of the two keys to 4-106.
* Stephania will not deign to notice low-level PCs, though evil characters or those who have helped other members of the Cult of Set might be brought to her attention.
	* Her favor could be won by performing tasks: defeating the demon in 4-58, reclaiming the Third Mystery of Set, etc.

Stephania (33%), Set pontifex (see new monsters), as a 10th-level female Archontean cleric of Set: SZ M; AL LE; AC 0; MV 120’, or 90’ with Set armor +2; HD 9+2; HP 66; #AT 1; Dmg 6-11 (mace +3), 3-6 (staff of withering); MR 15%. 
* Abilities: STR 17 (including +1 from her boots), INT 15, WIS 18, DEX 14, CON 11, CHA 16.
* She is +1 to hit and +1 to damage due to her strength.
* Possessions
	* footman’s mace +3; Set armor +2 (see Arden Vul items)
	* rod of wind control (see new magic items)
	* staff of withering (15 charges)
	* pontifex’s was stick (see new magic items)
	* a ring of Set named Batzas (see new magic items)
	* a necklace of missiles (one 7-dice, two 5-dice, and four 3-dice missiles)
	* boots of the ogre (see new magic items)
	* potions: truthfulness, deafening light (see new magic items for both)
	* scrolls: hallow, sun’s gift, warding chain of glyphs (see new spells for all three)
	* a platinum holy symbol of Set (250 gp)
	* a keyring with keys to most door locks within the precincts of Set, including the sole key to 4-51A, the keys to 3-110, one of the few keys to SL8-1 (aka EX-16), and one of the two keys to 4-106.
* Typically cleric spells: 
	* bless, command, cure light wounds (x2), detect good, detect magic; 
	* chant, hold person, know alignment, silence 15’ radius, augury, speak with animals; 
	* dispel magic, glyph of warding, curse, prayer; 
	* cause serious wounds (x2), protection from good 10’ radius, detect lie; 
	* commune, flame strike.
		* In certain circumstances, she may have prayed for quest and raise dead in her 5th-level slots.

##### 4-51a: Shrine to the Snake

* A long set of narrow stairs from the high priestess’s room leads to this unusual fane.
	* Unlike the rest of the level, this room is clad in blue marble flecked with white, and all corners are rounded (built in the era of Rudishva / Kaliyani alliance).
	* Lit sconces line the walls, providing good – if smoky – light.
	* Against the north wall is a 2’-high dais on which sits an enormous snake’s head, mouth open, revealing fangs.
		* Each eye is 3’ wide, composed of 128 faceted chrysoprase gems (50 gp each).
		* Secret Door (north): This door is located within the giant snake head, and is 
		* opened by 
		* Pulling one of the fangs opens a secret door within the snake's throat.
	* In the southwest corner is the encampment of a team of kaliyani sorcerers and their servants.
		* Two hammocks hung from rings in the walls, a tripod and pot over a fire-ring, and three 4’-tall dried mushrooms with hollowed caps and stems (containers).
		* Unless intruders are accompanied by Stephania, the kaliyani attack on sight.
			* If combat goes badly or them, they beat a fighting retreat through the northern secret door.
	* Secret Door (southwest): unknown any except the kaliyani, hard to locate (1 in 8), opened by pushing a slab of marble inward, then sliding it to the west.

GM Note
* Stephania was shocked fifteen years ago when a kaliyani digging party broke through the wall of 4-51.  Linking the snake-like kaliyani to one of Set’s favorite incarnations (the snake) was an easy way to establish an alliance, and the kaliyani were quick to recognize the potential value of such an alliance.
	* Over the past decade, the stairs linking 4-51 and 4-51a have been completed, and the shrine in 4-51a constructed.
	* The kaliyani have not told Stephania that they also completed a second set of stairs, with secret door, leading to area 4-39.
* As yet, no priest or priestess has visited the kaliyani compound, but the high priestess does take regular consultation with her allies about affairs on the lower levels.
	* Knowledge of this strange alliance is limited to High Priestess Stephania, Alexandros the Bibliothecarius (4-54), and Belisarius the Overseer (4-47).
	* Marius Junienos, Lacedaion of Archontos, and the Guildmasters of Service are merely aware that the high priestess has a private shrine. 

Plesstra, 7th-level kaliyani sorcerer (see new monsters), SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 150’ on six legs, 60’ upright; HD 7; HP 41; #AT 3; Dmg 2-5/2-5/6-24 (dagger/dagger/blasting rod). Special defenses: immune to poison and mind-affecting spells. Special: infravision. Psionic ability: 220. Attack modes psionic blast, mind thrust, psychic crush. Defense modes: mind blank, thought shield, intellect fortress. Disciplines: cellular adjustment, domination, detect magic; mind barring. Spells: comprehend languages, charm person, hypnotism; darkness 15’ 
radius, invisibility, mirror image; dispel magic. Possessions: bracers of defense (AC 5); kaliyani blasting rod, with 6 charges (see new technological items); two serrated daggers; 5 lb of arcanum (see new magic items); 14 small chrysoprase gems (60 gp each).

Nassiv, 5th-level kaliyani sorcerer (see new monsters): SZ M; AL LE; AC 6; MV 150’ on six legs, 60’ upright; HD 5; HP 32; #AT 2; Dmg 4-6/2-5 (dagger +2/dagger) or 2-7/2-7 (javelins). Special defenses: immune to poison and mind-affecting spells. Special: infravision. Psionic ability: 200. Attack modes: psionic blast, mind thrust. Defense modes mind blank, mental barrier. Disciplines: clairaudience, clairvoyance, invisibility, telepathic projection. Spells: charm person, dancing lights, hypnotic pattern. Possessions: potion of invisibility; potion of fire breath; one dagger +2 and a second normal dagger; 6 javelins; a silver ring with an ouroboros on it (275 gp), two gold torcs (150 gp each); 4 vials of kaliyani refreshening liquid (see Arden Vul items).

6 1st-level kaliyani soldiers (see new monsters): SZ M; AL LE; AC 6; MV 150’ on six legs, 60’ upright; HD 4; HP 29, 27, 26, 25, 24, 24; #AT 2 or 1; Dmg 1-4/1-4 or 3-8/3-8 (scimitars) 
and 2-7/2-7 (javelins). Special defenses: immune to poison and mind-affecting spells. Special: infravision. Possessions: twin serrated scimitars; six javelins; minor jewelry worth 33 gp. These individuals have no psionic ability. 

##### 4-51b: Stairs Down to the Kaliyani Pits (SL9-75)

* The secret door in the snake head leads to an oval tunnel with many steps leading down 650’ to the Kaliyani Pits (SL9-75).

### 4-52: Treasury

* Only the three high priests of the cult know of this secret treasury.
* 3 large open stone boxes contain:
	* 15,000 gp, 1,000 pp, and 50 gems of various types worth 100 gp each)
	* 6 pieces of elaborate ritual ware (100 gp per piece)
	* A helm of underwater action
	* A set of enchanted imperial field plate +1 (av items)
	* An oathbow (new)
	* A small locked and trapped (poison gas) iron box containing a complete deck of many things and a complete deck of the magi (new).

### 4-53: Square of the High Priest

* The deacons use this space as the nerve center of the cult of Set.
* The walls of this octagonal space are painted a cheerful yellow, while the rib-vaulted ceiling is sky-blue.
	* A globe shining continual light hangs from the center of the vaulting.
	* The northern half contains five desks and chairs, and a large worktable with benches.
		* Officials of the cult use this space to devise and carry out their political plots.
	* The southern half is open, with a huge set of blood-red drapes that cloak the entrance to the chapel (4-61).

8 bureaucrats, as Set cultists (see new monsters): SZ M; AL LE; AC 9; MV 90’; HD 1; HP 7, 6, 6, 5, 5, 4, 4, 3; #AT 1; Dmg 1-4 (dagger) or 2-7 (flail) or 1-6 (staff). Special attacks: fanaticism. Possessions: padded armor; daggers; flails or staves.

### 4-54: Bibliothecarius

* Alexandros the bibliothecarius (librarian) makes his quarters here. 
	* It is spartan, with a rumpled bed, a chest of clothing, and an escritoire with chair.
	* 25% chance he has brought an interesting volume from the library (4-55) to study.
* Alexandros is the typical doddering scholar; he lacks all interest in politics, a fact that has allowed him to maintain his position into his 80s.
	* He is genuinely interested in the history of Arden Vul and could be a useful source of information if cultivated (and if Stephania allowed it).
		* She might allow consultation with him in return for a favor or two).
	* Insights
		* The causes of the destruction of the city and the role of the Sortians and Theosophs in fomenting that debacle. 
		* Fragments of information suggesting the existence of a hidden Sortian (now, ‘Priscian’) complex under Arden Vul (i.e., 9-58 to 9-64).
* 33% chance he is present here, otherwise he is in the library (4-55).

Alexandros, male Archontean human scholar (33%): SZ M; AL LE; AC 10; MV 90’; HD 1-1; HP 6; #AT 1; Dmg 1-2 (metal stylus).

### 4-55: Library

* The leaders of the cult of Set have made a serious effort to reconstruct the formerly extensive library of Set.
	* Never as impressive as that of Thoth, the original library contained some important and rare texts.  The current collection is much less extensive and interesting.
	* Still, under the care of Alexandros, it is starting to be reassembled.
		* Alexandros is present 66% of the time.
* The vestibule to the library has several benches and pegs (for cloaks).
* The eastern third of the room is given over to reading desks and tables.
* The western two-thirds contain wooden shelves holding the collection.
	* Alexandros has his desk in the center of the stacks.
	* The collection contains 158 items in a variety of formats: large illuminated codices, small portable octavos, sets of scrolls in parchment or papyrus, even a few sets of bronze plaques held in silk-lined boxes.
	* Most of the volumes are recent, the sort of thing that one can still buy at higher-end booksellers in any of the large cities of the Empire: memoirs of imperial officials; official histories of the empire; general treatises on magic, theology, estate management, or monster ecology; medical treatises; recipes for potions and poisons; and so forth.
	* About 20% of the volumes are truly unique and worthy of interest.
		* The hagiographical The Lives of the Noble Founders, Arden and Vul
		* The Deeds of Marius Tricotor, by Lucius Cornelius Scriptor
		* A condensed one-volume version of the Tales of Larel One-Eye (see 3-46)
		* A badly corrupted version of Clarius’s On the Wars of the Old Ones with the Trolls, with (mis-)information on the rudishva
		* A quire of notes prepared by Alexandros himself entitled On the Location of Priscus Pulcher (books)
		* Justinian the Wise’s ancient A True History of Isadora, companion of Priscus Pulcher (with much disinformation)
		* The Song of Jacinth the Rose
		* Sardonyx Peridot’s Sorcerous Properties of Gems
		* The Value of Mud, by Herodian the Blessed
		* The Priscian A Canticle of Arcane Knowledge
		* Ysgred the Mad’s infamous Thirty Uses for Arcanum
		* Thorcin Poisons and their Cures
		* The Deeds of the Azure Knights
		* Ixion of Narsileon’s infamous The Nine Hells: a Catalogue with descriptions and summoning notes
		* 3 arcane spell books
			* Most level 1-2 magic user spells, nighteyes of Bastet, Pelagion’s bridge of sighs, Pelagion’s rock sympathy (new)
			* 1-6 other new spells (roll 1d8 for level; select from new spells).
		* A scroll bearing the addresses to three of the Thothian teleportation rings
			* GR-RE-YE-BL-BK-WH (AV-27)
			* WH-YE-BL-GR-RE-BK (2-19)
			* RE-BK-BL-GR-YE-WH (8-17).

### 4-56: Second Priest’s Chamber

* This is the chamber of Marius Junienos, the second priest of the cult of Set.
	* Marius’s chamber is elegantly, if not sumptuously, furnished. 
	* Painted screens set off a private area to the south.
		* A four-poster bed, easy chair and table, armoire, and cabinet.
			* The cabinet holds his collection of signet rings (32, taken from victims in his schemes, 10-1,000 gp each).
			* Over the bed hangs a magnificent tapestry of the imperial capital of Archontos in great detail (500 gp).
			* Attached to the underside of the bed, invisible, is his spell book.
			* Inside the armoire is a box (locked, trapped w / poison needle; 5,033 pp).
	* Marius’s working area is to the north.
		* Two writing desks, a scroll cabinet, a weapon/armor stand, and an uncomfortable set of wooden chairs around a small coffee table.
			* Along the walls are shelves holding 11 marble busts (100 gp each, heavy), mostly of members of Marius’s family, but also of former priests of Set.
				* One bust is enchanted; if told ‘speak’, it recites 4 off-color jokes in quick succession.
			* The coffee table has a solid gold coffee service (300 gp).
			* The weapons and armor are unused and for display only.
				* Set armor +2 (av items), a ceremonial spear of ebony (100 gp), a short sword +1
			* On the desk are valuable documents (GM’s choice).

Marius Junienos
* Second-in-command of the cult of Set, and a member of the Junienos clan, of the Five Families, thus an aristocrat of the highest rank.
	* His kinsmen have claimed Marius died in a fire, although a few (and the Imperial Drome) know the truth: that Marius is thoroughly evil and that he cares more for the restoration of the cult of Set than for kin or empire.
	* Though unscrupulous, Marius is completely loyal to Stephania, whose abilities and iron will he admires. 
* Marius is a thin, ascetic-looking man of middle age, with a long nose and receding hairline.
	* He wears a red robe blazoned with a black boar, red bracers of defense (AC 3), and a red cloth headdress shaped like a Set animal.
	* His bearing is aristocratic, with little patience with the slow or insipid.
	* Marius’s great skill lies in subtle political machinations, and he has numerous schemes in various stages of completion, both within the Halls and without.
		* He's the lead on dealing with Iskander?
	* Marius’s private wealth has helped prop up the cult, and Stephania values him enormously.
	* Marius loathes Anna Ligareon (4-8) and shows it by ignoring her completely.
	* Marius has a strong drug addiction of which no one save Galadnor Half-Elven (see 4-31) is aware, but it has not yet affected his abilities.

Marius Junienos (50%), Set pontifex (see new monsters), as a 9th-level male Archontean magic user: SZ M; AL LE; AC -1; MV 120’; HD 9; HP 29; #AT 1; Dmg 4-9 (staff of striking) or 
3-6 (dagger +2); MR 15%. Abilities: STR 9; INT 18; WIS 15; DEX 16; CON 10; CHA 12. 
* Possessions: robe, headdress, red bracers of defense (AC 3), staff of striking (23 charges), a dagger +2; a ring of three wishes (one remaining), a ring of Set named Fronto the Wise (see new magic items); potions of extra healing, fly, and gaseous form; a platinum holy symbol of Set (250 gp); and a key-ring with keys to SL8-1 and 4-106.
* Memorized spells: comprehend languages, charm person, magic missile, shield; continual light, detect good, mirror image, ESP; dispel magic, fly, suggestion; fear, polymorph other; feeblemind. 

Marius’s Spell Book: All 1st-level spells; audible glamer, continual light, detect good, darkness 15’ radius, detect invisibility, ESP, forget, Frigg’s elephant ears (see new spells), Frigg’s jelly legs (see new spells), invisibility, knock, levitate, locate object, magic mouth, mirror image, ray of enfeeblement, rope trick, stinking cloud, strength, web; blink, clairaudience, clairvoyance, dispel magic, fireball, fly, garrulous mouth (see new spells), gust of wind, haste, hold person, invisibility 10’ radius, lightning bolt, monster summoning I, Pelagion’s rock sympathy (see new spells), phantasmal force, slow, suggestion, water breathing; confusion, extension I, fear, ice storm, massmorph, minor globe of invulnerability, polymorph other, remove curse, wall of fire; conjure elemental, contact other plane, feeblemind, mage’s faithful hound, teleport.

### 4-57: Third Priest’s Chamber

* This is the chamber of Lacedaion of Archontos, the third priest of the cult of Set.
	* A private area is set off by painted screens to the south.
		* A plain bed, an armoire, an easy chair, a table, and a set of manacles and whips.
		* The south wall contains an enormous fresco painted on a wooden frame showing the black boar of Set consuming the sun.
		* In the armoire is a box (locked, trapped with a glyph of warding): 4 large keys, a periapt of proof against poison, four diamonds (500 gp each), and 273 gp.
	* A public area to the north. 
		* The public area has a writing desk, a scroll cabinet, a low table with three chairs, and an armor/weapon stand.
		* Three tapestries line the walls, showing scenes of ritual sacrifice and the domination of the weak.
		* On the stands are a pristine Set armor +2 (av items), spear +1, long sword +1.

Lacedaion of Archontos
* Brilliant but insecure, he harbors resentment about Marius’s aristocratic status.
* Belisarius the Overseer has been trying to persuade Lacedaion that Stephania has been slighting him.
	* Although aware of Belisarius’s antipathy for the high priestess, Lacedaion’s vanity and resentment have pushed him a bit further along the path of treason than his intellect would normally allow.
* Lacedaion is a short, dark man with a stylish goatee, piercing eyes, and a scar running along his left cheek.
	* He wears flashy and extravagant red velvet robes at almost all times, eschewing his formal Set armor +2 unless preparing for a fight.

Lacedaion (50%), Set pontifex (see new monsters), as a 9th-level male Archontean cleric of Set: SZ M; AL LE; AC 2 (without armor) or 0 (with Set armor +2); MV 120’, or 90’ with Set armor +2; HD 9; HP: 60; #AT 1; Dmg 4-9 (mace +2); MR 15%. Abilities: STR 12; INT 17; WIS 17; DEX 14; CON 12; CHA 15.
* Possessions: red velvet robes with bracers of defense (AC 5), or Set armor +2 (see Arden Vul items); footman’s mace +2; ring of protection +2; wand of negation (12 charges); a ring of Set named Sittas (see new magic items); an amulet of proof against detection or location; a potion of extra healing; a platinum holy symbol of Set (250 gp); and a key-ring with keys to SL8-1 and 4-106.
* Spells prayed for: bless, command, cause light wounds, cure light wounds, light, sanctuary; chant, detect charm, hold person, know alignment, resist fire, silence 15’ radius; animate dead, blindness, dispel magic, glyph of warding; cure serious wounds, protection from good 10’ radius; insect plague.

### 4-58: Blocked Passage and Dangerous Room

* Several bits of broken column block the hallway outside this door (locked).
	* Glued to one fragment is a large note (Archontean): “No access per order of High Priestess Stephania.”
	* Close listeners at the door hear a whispered suggestion (Archontean): “Help me. I am so lonely. I will be your friend.”  Save versus spells or believe the voice and try to open the door.
	* The chamber contains a succubus, still posing problems for Stephania and her cult.
		* The door has a powerful protection against evil spell on it, refreshed every week via an elaborate ceremony.  It is secured against teleportation and ethereal travel.
* This former administrative chamber hosts a dozen desks and tables, as well as a row of scroll and map cabinets.
	* A scattering of 18 gp can be collected after two turns of searching.
	* Among tedious administrative documents (lists of supplies, payments, etc.) are 2 scrolls (cone of cold; knit bones (new)), and a charter sealed by Stephania (4-51).
		* The charter promises a bounty of 200 gp per varumani head to a certain Kallion the White (see 8-15).  It could be used to convince the troll thegn (7-30) to aid in a protracted campaign against Set.
	* Pinned to an overturned desk is a haiku recited by a guardsman who had received a vision from Set.
		* "Unguents piled on high, Bones wrapped and entombed, There Theskelon rests." (it refers to the tomb of Theskelon, 4-142).
		* The deacons who recorded it did not recognize its significance before they were driven from the chamber.
	* Secret Door (north, to 4-59, locked): Stephania (4-51) holds the sole key.

* Currently home to a succubus calling herself Maris, accidentally summoned by Herbert, a (former) deacon of Set.
	* She is bound to the chamber and to the body of the unfortunate deacon, who she  delights in impersonating via her shape change ability.
	* She slew the deacons Stephania sent to handle her and turned them into wights.
	* Although she has enjoyed the game of torment with the priesthood of Set, Maris is deeply annoyed at her imprisonment.  She is eager to escape in order to wreak chaos in the Forum.
	* The wights are mindless, but they obey Maris as long as they are within sight of her.

Maris the succubus, posing as Herbert the deacon: SZ M; AL CE; AC 0; MV 120’, 180’ flying (Class C); HD 6; HP 40; #AT 2; Dmg 1-3/1-3; MR 70%. Constant abilities: infravision. Special attacks: energy drain; charm person; suggestion. Special defenses: +1 or better weapons to hit; half damage from cold, electricity, fire, and gas. Special: cause darkness 5’; become ethereal; ESP; clairaudience; shape change; gate (40% chance).
* Possessions: sword +2, chaos blade (new) 

3 wights: SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 4+3; HP 33, 29, 27; #AT 1; Dmg 1-4. Special attacks: energy drain. Special defenses: silver or magic needed to hit; immune to sleep, charm, hold, cold, poison, and paralysis.

### 4-59: Shadowy Trouble

* A pack of shadows occupy this unfinished chamber.
	* It was only partially excavated when disaster struck Arden Vul; the shadows are the remains of slaves entombed here when the priests of Set fled.
	* The east wall was painted a rough, but clear painting of Set in his Set animal form.
		* It was debased by the dying slaves, who scrawled (in various tongues) “Murderer!”, “Lord of Deceit”, and so forth.
	* The once brightly-painted south wall of the chamber now shows only smears of blood and other foul fluids.  The floor is paved except for a 3’ belt of unfinished stone along the west wall.
	* The river flows east through an extremely swift and narrow tunnel only 4’ in diameter (passage would batter for 6d10, before emerging at 4-68).
	* A war hammer +1 lies in the debris.
		* Its handle is broken and requires 100 gp of work by a high-quality smith.
	* Secret Door (south, to 4-58, locked): easy to detect (1 in 4) due to the hammer marks that cover it.  The sole key is held by High Priestess Stephania (4-51).
* Lying on the pavement are the long-rotted, desiccated, and sometimes gnawed remains of the entombed.
	* Amid the bones of one is a short written testimonial (in Goblin Runic) describing the last days of the slaves.

14 shadows: SZ M; AL CE; AC 7; MV 120; HD 3+3; HP 24, 23, 22, 21, 20(x3), 19(x3), 18, 18, 17, 16; #AT 1; Dmg 2-5. Special attacks: STR drain. Special defenses: 90% undetectable; +1 or 
better weapons to hit; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and cold. 

### 4-60: Elite Guards

* Eight fanatical elite temple guards under the personal command of Stephania reside here.
	* The guardsmen and their sergeant sleep in bunk beds and possess a trestle table, bench, water barrel, a row of pegs for cloaks and equipment, several armor racks, a shared chest, and a dartboard.
		* Each guard has a stash of 10d10 sp.
	* A large mural shows the Long Stair (4-19) and a company of Set Guardsmen escorting a variety of prisoners.
		* Inspection shows the faces of the prisoners are individualized, including one that looks very much like Belisarius the Overseer (4-47).
			* These reflect the true enemies of this sept of guardsmen, past and present.
			* If the party is an enemy of the cult, the GM might decide that one of the PCs’ faces appears on the mural.
* Most of the time only four guardsmen are present here.

4 elite Set guardsmen (see new monsters), as 3rd-level Archontean fighters: SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 60’; HD 3; HP 26, 25, 25, 24; #AT 1, Dmg 2-7 (mace), 1-6 (spear) and 1-4 (light crossbow). Special defense: fanaticism.
* Possessions: red scale mail and wooden shield; footman’s maces; spears; light crossbows with 20 bolts.
* One of the men has an ivory olifant (75 gp). 

Sergeant Triforius (50%), the Set sergeant (see new monsters), as a 5th-level Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL LE; AC 3; MV 60’; HD 5; HP 43; #AT 1, Dmg 3-8 (mace +1), 1-6 (spear) and 1-4 (light crossbow). Special defense: fanaticism.
* Possessions: Set armor (see Arden Vul items) and wooden shield; footman’s mace +1; spear; light crossbow with 20 bolts and 3 bolts of fire (see new magic items).

## Level 4: 61 - 75

### 4-61: Chapel of Set

* This is the private chapel to Set used by the senior priests and deacons of the cult.
	* A barrel-vaulted, brick-lined ceiling rises 25’ above the floor; the walls are covered by heavy red drapes.
		* The western transept, hidden by the drapery, has a huge oil portrait of Stephania (4-51), as well as two chairs and a table, on which sits a scrying ball (new) keyed to the Forum of Set (4-2).
		* The east transept, hidden by drapery, holds a guard chamber, where four of the elite temple guards from 4-60 wait.
	* At the south end of the chapel is an obsidian altar stained with blood, on which rest an ancient obsidian knife, a copper bowl and a copper goblet (250 gp for all).
		* Hidden compartment in the altar (trapped with poison gas): the boar’s helm, a lesser artifact of Set (new).  The current cult is ignorant of the helm.
	* Secret Door (in eastern corridor, leading to 4-36): This door is 4’x2.5’ in size, and difficult to locate (1 in 8). It opens to those who knock four times in rapid succession on the door. The current Set cult is ignorant of this door. 
* The chapel exudes a strong aura of evil (evil beings save at +2, good beings at -2).
	* Set is also more likely to hear invocations to him in this chamber and to send a lesser devil to aid his supplicants.
* 25% chance a ritual is taking place; if so, it involves High Priestess Stephania and two Set deacons.

4 elite Set guardsmen (see new monsters), as 3rd-level Archontean fighters: SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 60’; HD 3; HP 26, 25, 25, 24; #AT 1, Dmg 2-7 (mace), 1-6 (spear) and 1-4 (light crossbow). Special defense: fanaticism. Possessions: red scale mail and wooden shield; footman’s maces; spears; light crossbows with 20 bolts.

1-2 Set deacons (see new monsters), as 6th-level Archontean clerics of Set (25% chance): SZ M; AL LE; AC 3; MV 90’; HD 6; HP 39, 36; #AT 1; Dmg 3-8 (mace +1). Possessions: Set 
armor +1 (see Arden Vul items); deacon’s was stick (see new magic items); footman’s mace +1; an amulet of protection against normal missiles (see new magic items); a potion of extra healing; a potion of glibness; a scroll of curse; and a gold holy symbol of Set (150 gp). Spells prayed for: command, cure light wounds (x2), cause fear, protection from good; chant, hold person, know alignment, resist fire, silence 15’ radius; animate dead, dispel magic, cause blindness; cause serious wounds.

(25%) High Priestess Stephania; for stats, see 4-51.

### 4-62: Sorcerous Ally

* The magic user Pelagion the Grey lives in this hidden chamber.
	* A simple cot, a tripod of heating (new), two chests (wizard locked), a barrel of wine, two boxes of dried foodstuffs, and an adequately-equipped laboratory (5000 gp) which Belisarius found intact when he discovered this chamber.
		* Chest #1: Pelagion’s spell book, five blank scrolls, and a scroll (Pelagion’s bridge of sighs, new), the spell book of Visby.
			* Visby was a mage caught in the Forum spying for the Drome, traded to the lizardmen of SL5. He is currently languishing at SL5-34.
		* Chest #2: A full stock of alchemical ingredients and material components (1,000 gp total), 8 doses of arcanum jelly (new), a glass activation squares (black and yellow).
* Pelagion has two hellhounds for company and protection.

Pelagion the Grey
* Pelagion is young (35), but exposure to arcanum has caused unusually deep age-lines on his face and a premature change in hair color (to snowy white).
* Pelagion is studying the arcanum deposit in 4-63, allegedly to provide Belisarius (4-47) with an edge against Stephania (4-51), but really to further his own arcane interests.
	* He has been living here for a year studying the substance. 
	* He recognizes the potential dangers of extended exposure to arcanum and has taken to breaking off chunks of the stuff for study in the relative safety of 4-62.
* He hops around with manic energy on one leg (the other is withered) and loves nothing more than to expound on the many benefits of arcanum.
	* In a stroke of arcanum-fueled inspiration, he has developed 2 new spells (recorded in his spell book) and a formula for a potion that temporarily enhances INT (clarity), not written down for fear of theft.
	* In addition physical scars of his time with arcanum, he has become increasingly eccentric: talking to himself in bizarre languages both real and fantastic, licking rock in an (unsuccessful) effort to determine its taste and properties, and generally acting in an unstable way.
* If approached from the north (the caves), he appears cautious but eager to trade knowledge about arcanum.  If approached from the south without Belisarius, he is hostile.

Pelagion the Grey, 6th-level male Archontean magic user: SZ M; AL LE; AC 7; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 19; #AT 1; Dmg 2-5 (dagger +1). Abilities: STR 11, INT 17, WIS 13, DEX 17, CON 10, CHA 12. Possessions: dagger +1; wand of frost (33 charges); ring of spell turning; potion of gaseous form; potions of clarity(x3) (see new magic items). Spells memorized: sleep, shield, magic missile, charm person; mirror image, invisibility; monster summoning I, slow.
* 57 gp, dagger +1, wand of frost (33 charges), ring of spell turning, potion of gaseous form, and 3 potions of clarity (new).

### 4-63: Arcanum Cave

* This rocky cave is home to a large deposit of arcanum (new).
	* Center of the cave is completely formed of crystalline growths, causing the entire area to glow with a sickly orange light.
	* Pelagion the Grey (4-62) is studying the arcanum.
	* A wooden stool stands in the center of the formation; a mallet and several fragments lie to one side.
* The arcanum cave exerts certain compulsions on magic users and illusionists, as usual. 

### 4-64: Hidden Prison

* Accessible from the secret door in 4-9, this is the secret prison used by the Guildmasters of the Guild of Service for their most important political prisoners.
	* The cave floor has been smoothed and sanded.
	* Eight sets of steel restraints have been driven into the walls.
	* A wooden bench and table, with a set of wooden cups and a copper ewer sit in the center of the room.
* At the moment the prison is occupied by three persons:
	* The real Gunnar, Guildmaster of the Guild of Service, imprisoned here when the doppelgangers took his place (see 4-10).
		* If rescued, Gunnar quickly becomes imperious, demanding his return to the main cult centers, offering a minimal reward but immunity from prosecution.
	* Kaledon, a deacon of Set, seized by the real Gunnar several months ago for interrogation.
		* Kaledon is obsequious, offering to serve his rescuers (planning to betray them to recover his favor in the cult).
	* Callista, a good-aligned fighter apprehended by the Guild after discovering she had been sent by the Imperial Drome to investigate the cult.
		* Callista will accompany good-aligned parties.

Gunnar, Master of the Guild of Service, 10th-level male Wiskin thief: SZ M; AL LE; AC 7; MV 120’; HD 10; HP 18 (max 48); #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 17, INT 14, WIS 12, DEX 17, CON 14, CHA 13. Thief skills: PP 85%, OL 77%, F/RT 65%, MS 83%, HS 68%, HN 30%, CW 99%, RL 50%. Possessions: none.

Kaledon, a Set deacon (see new monsters), as a 6th-level Archontean cleric of Set: SZ M; AL LE; AC 10; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 8 (max 37); #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 12, INT 12, WIS 17, DEX 9, CON 10, CHA 14. Kaledon has no possessions, nor has he been able to pray for spells.

Callista, 4th-level female Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL CG; AC 10; MV 120’; HD 4; HP 12 (max 41); #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 17, INT 10, WIS 11, DEX 13, CON 17, CHA 15.

### 4-65: Sink Hole and Whirlpool

* The river ends in a huge sink hole and whirlpool.
	* A ledge 15’ up the south side overlooks the maelstrom and leads to the secret prison (4-64).
	* The sink hole descends 100’ through rocky passages to 5-103.
		* Those swept into the whirlpool will surely drown unless protected by magic

### 4-66: Lizard Cavern and Cliff

* This large cavern marks the northern boundary of the cult of Set's control (in the old days they dominated the caverns beyond).
	* Numerous small lizards (1’-2’ long) and pale, white cave flitters (like dragonflies) make their home in the crannies that line the walls of the cave.
	* A river runs down the middle of the cavern, with a stone bridge crossing it.
		* The slender span gracefully arches over the river, 6’ wide and rising 10’ above the river. Sconces at each end hold burning torches. 
	* On the north side of the river ae small patches of giant and regular mushrooms, as well as large patches of lichen on the walls.
	* A 40’-tall cliff lies on the south side of the river, its top connected to the cave floor by a steep ramp.
		* A patrol of Set guardsmen armed with crossbows lurks at the top of the southern cliff.
		* If engaged by strong forces, the acolyte blows an olifant to summon assistance from 4-45 and 4-46.
	* At the western end of the cavern is a 40’ waterfall, as well as another 40’-tall cliff.

4 Set guardsmen (see new monsters), as 2nd-level Archontean fighters: SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 60’; HD 2; HP 18, 17, 15, 12; #AT 1, Dmg 2-7 (mace), 1-6 (spear) and 1-4 (light crossbow). Special defense: fanaticism. Possessions: red scale mail and wooden shield; footman’s maces; spears; light crossbows with 20 bolts.

1 Set acolyte (see new monsters), as a 3rd-level Archontean cleric of Set: SZ M; AL LE; AC 4; MV 60’; HD 3; HP 19; #AT 1; Dmg 2-7 (mace) and 1-4 (light crossbow). Possessions: Set 
armor (see Arden Vul items); footman’s mace; light crossbow; acolyte’s was stick (see new magic items); and a silver holy symbol of Set (10 gp). Spells prayed for: command, cure light wounds, curse (reverse of bless), protection from good; hold person, silence 15’ radius.

### 4-67: Rushing River

* The river is formed from two smaller streams that join at the western edge of the cavern (4-66).
	* The river is 10’ deep and boasts a strong current. Anyone falling in has a good chance of being pulled to their death at 4-65.

### 4-68: Cavern with Hole

* This large cavern is a side-cavern of 4-66, with a branch of the subterranean river flowing through it.
	* The air is cool and moist, and numerous colonies of mold and lichen grow here.  Large numbers of cave crickets inhabit the cavern.
	* A 10’-diameter hole in the cave floor drops 15’ down to the ceiling of the tunnel running between 4-72 and 4-90.
		* It provides access for the subterranean lizards (4-72) that hunt crickets here. 

2 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 42, 38; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 4-69: Fallen Statue

* A the center of this 25’-tall sandy-floored cavern protrudes the stump of a broken statue (4’ of legs, twined in a robe).
	* Some shapeless lumps of stone nearby are probably the rest of the statue.
	* Digging into the sand to find the statue’s base, reveals a circular pavement 12’ in diameter set with a beautiful mosaic of pastoral subterranean scenes: lizards, mushrooms, bats, sarcophagi, altars, etc.
	* The base of the statue reads (Mithric): “Chibalba, lord of the Deeps, watches over these caves. Summon him if thy need is great.”
* Chibalba, guardian of the underworld, was also in antiquity associated with subterranean life and protection.
	* Standing on the mosaic and reciting Chibalba’s name three times in a row, or declaiming “I summon thee, Chibalba!”, calls his avatar (once per month).
	* It speaks (Mithric), describing the aid it will lend (depends on the invoker's need) in a solemn, deep voice, then does not speak again.
	* If invoked by a cleric of Chibalba, all four types of aid are proffered, with the combat avatar serving the cleric for one whole day.
* Note: Two other identical (and more intact) statues of Chibalba appear at 8-66 and 9-87.

Situation Aid Offered
* In combat: Avatar fights for duration of one combat: AC 0, HD 8, HP 58, #AT 1, damage 1-10
* Badly wounded: Cure critical wounds x2
* Lightly wounded: Cure serious wounds x2
* Uninjured: Detect traps, infravision, and locate place (new) for 10 turns

### 4-70: Warning Sign

* A human wearing only a filthy loincloth has been crucified upside down on the north wall of this T-intersection.
	* His eyes have been plucked out, and his flesh is badly gnawed.
	* On the wall next to him, scrawled in blood (Archontean), “The fate of runaways!”
* 33% chance that a subterranean lizard (4-72) is feeding on the corpse.

1 subterranean lizard (33% chance): SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 39; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 4-71: Subterranean Lizards

* Two large subterranean lizards forage in this otherwise nondescript cave.

2 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 38, 36; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 4-72: Lair of the Subterranean Lizards

* This is the primary lair of the pack of subterranean lizards that forages in the local caves. 
	* Along the east wall is a hollow that collects limey, but potable, water.
	* The floor is sandy, with four knobs ranging from 3’ to 6’ in height.
	* Around the knobs are a total of 15 small individual nests.
		* One nest has a clutch of 5 eggs (100 gp alive, to the right buyer). 
* 1d4+2 subterranean lizards are present at any time, at least one on the ceiling.  They will use the knobs as cover for ambush.

3-6 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 45, 43, 41, 39, 37, 35; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 4-73: Devoured Corpses

* Three partially devoured corpses lie in this crossroads.
	* A Set guardsman, armor broken and useless next to him.
		* A pouch with a moss agate (20 gp) and 26 sp, is hidden by his broken helmet.
	* Two adventurers, a half-elf ranger and a human magic user.
		* 10 arrows +2; pouch of gold dust (25 gp); bone scroll (blink, water breathing,  Basil’s torch treatment (new)).
	* All weapons are gone. 
* 50% chance 1d2 subterranean lizards are present.

1-2 subterranean lizards (50% chance): SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 41, 36; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 4-74: Heqeti Outpost

* The heqeti have recently restored this ancient watch post.
	* The rough walls are coated in glistening slime and starting to exhibit the pebbled texture of heqeti areas of the Halls.
	* To the southeast is one of the great pukel-manders (new).
	* The northwest contains a heqeti teleport well.
		* A 7’-diameter circle of stone, rising 3’ above the floor, containing inky blackness. Jumping in, one emerges seconds later at 10-24.
	* The narrow western tunnel leads to the river, opening 15’ above the river itself.
	* Secret Door (north): opens as a stuck door.
* Four heqeti hoppers are stationed here, gathering intelligence about this part of the Halls.

4 heqeti hoppers (see new monsters), as 4th-level fighters: SZ M; AL CE; AC 5; MV 60’, 150’ swimming; HD 4; HP 28, 26, 24, 22; #AT 2; Dmg 2-7 (spear), 1-6 (bite). Special attacks: hop; +1 to damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and water/ice.

##### 4-74a: Dead End Cave?

* A set of rough-carved stairs leads up from 4-73 to this small cave.
	* A slightly oily film glistening on the cave walls
	* A pair of ancient, human skeletons lies manacled together at wrist and feet.
* Secret Door (south): hard to find (1 in 8), opened by pulling (into 4-74a) with an open doors check.

### 4-75: Escaped Slaves

* This cave is quite damp, with moisture-slick walls but no standing water.
	* Several former slaves have escaped from the cult of Set and taken up temporary residence in this large cave.
		* Hearing rumors of a successful escape some years before (see 4-100), they headed north towards the ‘promised land’.  They are ‘pretty sure’ that there is safe haven there, but have been unable to find it.
		* The ex-slaves have only managed to kill a few lizards over the past week, and are hungry, thirsty, and quite desperate.
		* Among the group they have two daggers and one short sword, but no armor.
		* Knowledge
			* They know of the tunnel at 4-76, but don’t want to descend deeper, it's not the route to the promised land that was described to them.
			* They can describe 4-66, but won’t venture, fearing the Set patrols.
			* They suspect another exit (4-88) lies nearby, but haven’t found it yet and are divided whether to pursue it or the legendary promised land.
			* They are terrified of the owlbears, who have killed two of their number.

2-5 humans, escaped from the slave pits of the cult of Set.
* At the GM’s will some of these might be classed NPCs or men at arms.

* A pool of clear water on the eastern side draws many denizens of the caves, particularly the owlbears (75% for 1-2 owlbears).
	* Lots of small, ordinary lizards live here; their constant movement perhaps distracting.

### 4-82: Empty Cavern

* A high-ceilinged cavern with a sandy floor filled with indistinct tracks, some taloned and some booted.

	* The dried molt skin of an enormous snake (25’ long) is attached to a spear thrust into the sand.  It flutters in the gentle breeze that blows towards 4-88.
	* A reek of rot and excrement wafts on the breeze from the west (originating in 4-81).
	* Digging in the sand turns up the rusted remains of an ancient battle: 1-6 ruined weapons and 1-8 bits of unusable armor.

### 4-83: Small Cave

* This cave is rocky, uneven, and difficult to traverse, appearing as a dead end at first.

### 4-84: Set Watchpoint

* The face of a severe man is carved in the northern ell of this cave.
	* Motion within 20' causes a magic mouth to bark (Archontean) “Who goes there?”
	* The eyes convey images to the guard chamber at 4-45 (they don't have darkvision).
	* With this clairvoyance, a patrol of Set guardsmen arrives within 3 turns to investigate intruders.
		* 10% chance a patrol is already on its way, and arrives within 2-4 rounds.

4 Set guardsmen (see new monsters), as 2nd-level Archontean fighters: SZ M; AL LE; AC 5; MV 60’; HD 2; HP 18, 17, 15, 12; #AT 1, Dmg 2-7 (mace), 1-6 (spear) and 1-4 (light crossbow).
